
#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/0misc/Flash.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==0)
    {
        if(frame==5)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

}

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/0weap/bosser.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==31)
    {

    void vSelf = getlocalvar("self");
if(frame==1)
{
      fademusic(2, "data/music/duked1.ogg", 0, 0);
}
    if(frame==1){
      void vEntity;                                     //Target entity placeholder.
      int  iEntity;                                     //Entity enumeration holder.
      int  iType;                                       //Entity type.
      int  iHP;                                         //Entity HP
      int  iMax = openborvariant("count_entities");     //Entity count.

       //Enumerate and loop through entity collection.
      for(iEntity=0; iEntity<iMax; iEntity++){    
        vEntity = getentity(iEntity);                 //Get target entity from current loop.
        iType   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "type"); //Get target type.
        iHP   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "health"); //Get target health

        //Enemy type?
        if(iType == openborconstant("TYPE_ENEMY") && iHP > 0){
          damageentity(vEntity, vEntity, 2000, 1, openborconstant("ATK_NORMAL50"));
        }
      } 
      changeopenborvariant("slowmotion", 1);
    }
    if(frame==2){
      void self = getlocalvar("self");
      changeopenborvariant("slowmotion", 0);
      killentity(self);
    }
        return;
    }

}

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/1ndra/ndra.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==37)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            changeentityproperty(getlocalvar("self"), "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==38)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==39)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            Pause(0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==40)
    {

void self = getlocalvar("self"); //get the self var
void power = getentityproperty(self,"mp"); // get target's current mp
changeentityproperty(self, "mp", power+1); 
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==45)
    {

void self = getlocalvar("self"); //get the self var
void power = getentityproperty(self,"mp"); // get target's current mp
changeentityproperty(self, "mp", power+1); 
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==46)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN3"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==47)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN3"));
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN4"));
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN7"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==48)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN3"));
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN4"));
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_ATTACK4"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN7"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==50)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW1"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN3"));
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW1"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN4"));
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            ani0020(openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW1"), openborconstant("ANI_PAIN7"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==54)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            toss0001(110);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==55)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            toss0001(140);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==62)
    {

  if(frame==0){
    void self = getlocalvar("self");
    void target = getentityproperty(self, "opponent");

    setlocalvar("Target" + self, target);
  }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==68)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            slamstart();
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            antiwall2(-30, 20, 0);
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            position(2, 14, 5, -1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            position(5, -10, 20, -1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            position(5, -10, 20, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            depost(0);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            throw(10, 4, 0.6, 1.4, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }

}

# data/chars/0misc/ssfd.txt
########################################
void main()

    if(frame==1){

      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_wall", 0);
    }
    if(frame==7){
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 0);
    }
    if(frame==46){
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 1);
    }
        if(frame==7)
        {
            jump001(0.1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==7)
        {
            velo001(0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==46)
        {
            jump001(0.8, 1.1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==48)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==2067)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 0);
    }
        if(frame==9)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==2068)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 0);
    }
        if(frame==9)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==2069)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 1);
    }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

}

void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");

    if(animhandle==2438)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self"); //Get calling entity
    void Parent = getentityproperty(self, "parent");
    void P1 = getplayerproperty(0, "entity");
    void P2 = getplayerproperty(1, "entity");    
    int Dir = getentityproperty(self,"direction");
    int x = getentityproperty(self,"x");
    int z = getentityproperty(self,"z");

    if(P1 && frame>7){
      int PIndex = getentityproperty(Parent,"playerindex");
      void P1Anim = getentityproperty(P1, "animationID");
      void P2Anim = getentityproperty(P2, "animationID");
      void Model = getentityproperty(P1, "model");
      int P1x = getentityproperty(P1,"x");
      int P1z = getentityproperty(P1,"z");
      int P2x = getentityproperty(P2,"x");
      int P2z = getentityproperty(P2,"z");

      if(P1x-x<=14 && P1x-x>=-14 && P1z-z<=5 && P1z-z>=-5 && Model=="Billy" && ( P1Anim == openborconstant("ANI_IDLE") || P1Anim == openborconstant("ANI_WALK") && P2Anim != openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW58") )){
        changeentityproperty(P1, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
        changeentityproperty(P1, "animation", openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW58"));
        killentity(self);
      }

void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==2542)
    {
        if(frame==1)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==2543)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 1);
    }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==2544)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_gravity", 1);
    }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

}

            conditionalflip3();
        }
        if(frame==49)

            conditionalflip3();
        }
        return;
    }

        if(frame==2)
        {
            velo001(0.1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            velo001(0.0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            velo001(-0.1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            velo001(-0.2, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==6)
        {
            velo001(-0.3, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==7)
        {
            velo001(-0.2, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            velo001(-0.1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==9)
        {
            velo001(0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==10)

            velo001(0.1, 0, 0);

        if(frame==11)

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/0weap/slowitm.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==4132)
    {

    void vSelf = getlocalvar("self");
if(frame==1)
{
      fademusic(0.2, "data/music/silence.ogg", 0, 0);

    if(frame==1){
      void vEntity;                                     //Target entity placeholder.
      int  iEntity;                                     //Entity enumeration holder.
      int  iType;                                       //Entity type.
      int  iHP;                                         //Entity HP
      int  iMax = openborvariant("count_entities");     //Entity count.

       //Enumerate and loop through entity collection.
      for(iEntity=0; iEntity<iMax; iEntity++){    
        vEntity = getentity(iEntity);                 //Get target entity from current loop.
        iType   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "type"); //Get target type.
        iHP   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "health"); //Get target health

        //Enemy type?
        if(iType == openborconstant("TYPE_ENEMY") && iHP > 0){
          damageentity(vEntity, vEntity, 2000, 1, openborconstant("ATK_NORMAL49"));
        }
      } 
      changeopenborvariant("slowmotion", 0);
    }


}        if(frame==0)
        {
            spawn001("slow", "slow", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            spawn001("slow2", "slow2", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            spawn001("slow3", "slow3", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            spawn001("sentkiller", "sentkiller", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }

}

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/2duke/dukeU8.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==5192)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Gravity", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Wall", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MinZ", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MaxZ", 0);
    }
    if(frame==1){
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Gravity", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Wall", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MinZ", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MaxZ", 1);
    }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5194)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");

    if(frame==0){
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Gravity", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Wall", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MinZ", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MaxZ", 0);
    }
    if(frame==1){
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Gravity", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_Wall", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MinZ", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "Subject_to_MaxZ", 1);
    }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5195)
    {
        if(frame==22)
        {
            spawn001("dukeres1", "dukeres1", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==23)
        {
            spawn001("dminion", "dminion", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5204)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5209)
    {
        if(frame==4)
        {
            shadow(10, 10, 60, 4, 2, 180, 180, 180);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5212)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            slamstart2();
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            antiwall2(40, -40, 0);
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            position(1, 25, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            antiwall2(40, -40, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            position(2, 24, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            antiwall2(40, -40, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            position(4, 23, 5, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            position(1, 25, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            position(2, 24, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            position(4, 23, 5, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==6)
        {
            position(1, 25, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==7)
        {
            position(2, 24, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            position(4, 23, 5, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==9)
        {
            position(1, 25, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==10)
        {
            position(2, 24, 2, -0.1, 0);
        }
        if(frame==11)
        {
            depost(0);
        }
        if(frame==11)
        {
            finish(15, 1, -1.5, 1.5, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5214)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            velo001(1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            velo001(1.7, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            velo001(0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5226)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            jump001(1, -0.5, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5227)
    {
        if(frame==3)
        {
            vPro001("knife02", 0, 0, 40, 0, 3, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==5270)
    {
        if(frame==9)
        {
            conditionalflip3();
        }
        if(frame==34)
        {
            conditionalflip3();
        }
        if(frame==36)
        {
            conditionalflip3();
        }
        return;
    }

}

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/Bgs/dojo/tboxz.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==5483)
    {

    if(frame==1){
      void vEntity;                                     //Target entity placeholder.
      int  iEntity;                                     //Entity enumeration holder.
      int  iType;                                       //Entity type.
      int  iHP;                                         //Entity HP
      int  iMax = openborvariant("count_entities");     //Entity count.

       //Enumerate and loop through entity collection.
      for(iEntity=0; iEntity<iMax; iEntity++){    
        vEntity = getentity(iEntity);                 //Get target entity from current loop.
        iType   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "type"); //Get target type.
        iHP   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "health"); //Get target health

        //Enemy type?
        if(iType == openborconstant("TYPE_NONE") && iHP > 0){
          damageentity(vEntity, vEntity, 2000, 1, openborconstant("ATK_NORMAL50"));
        }
      } 
      changeopenborvariant("slowmotion", 0);
    }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            changeentityproperty(getlocalvar("self"), "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            changeentityproperty(getlocalvar("self"), "direction", 0);
        }

    void vSelf = getlocalvar("self");
if(frame==1)
{
      fademusic(0.5, "data/music/ZELDA.ogg", 1,1);
}        return;
    }

}

{

    if(frame==1){
      void vEntity;                                     //Target entity placeholder.

      int  iEntity;                                     //Entity enumeration holder.
      int  iType;                                       //Entity type.
      int  iHP;                                         //Entity HP
      int  iMax = openborvariant("count_entities");     //Entity count.

       //Enumerate and loop through entity collection.
      for(iEntity=0; iEntity<iMax; iEntity++){    
        vEntity = getentity(iEntity);                 //Get target entity from current loop.
        iType   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "type"); //Get target type.
        iHP   = getentityproperty(vEntity, "health"); //Get target health

        //Enemy type?
        if(iType == openborconstant("TYPE_NONE") && iHP > 0){
          damageentity(vEntity, vEntity, 2000, 1, openborconstant("ATK_NORMAL50"));
        }
      } 
      changeopenborvariant("slowmotion", 0);
    }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            changeentityproperty(getlocalvar("self"), "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            changeentityproperty(getlocalvar("self"), "direction", 0);
        }

    void vSelf = getlocalvar("self");
if(frame==1)
{
      fademusic(0.5, "data/music/NINJAG2.ogg", 1, 59535);
}        if(frame==15)
        {
            spawn001("tbox8", "tbox8", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }

}
